Carnatic music is mainly one of the two main sub-genres of Indian Raga music, which emerged out of Hindu foundation. It is rich in Raga and Tala. The main emphasis in Carnatic music is on vocal music; however, they are also presented instrumentally. 

For the connoisseurs of this sub-genre of Indian Music, INRECO has come forward with a rich palette of vocal and instrumental pieces by some of the accomplished artistes of Carnatic Music. 

There are Devi Krithis, Varnams, Thillanas, along with compositions of Thyagaraja, Swathi Thirunal. From Bombay.S.Jayashree, P.Unnikrishnan to Kadri Gopalnath, this channel is dedicated to the propagation of Carnatic music where INRECO family has been able to become a remarkable part in spreading the rich nuances of Carnatic music in particular.
